## Diagram 2

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class Crawl {
        +run()
        +load_config()
    }
    class Crawler {
        +crawl()
        +parse()
    }
    class Sync {
        +sync()
        +push()
    }
    class Backend {
        +store()
        +retrieve()
    }
    class Agent {
        +start()
        +stop()
    }
    class SDK {
        +client()
        +request()
    }
    Crawl <|-- Crawler
    Crawl o-- Sync
    Crawl --> Backend : uses
    Agent --> Crawl : orchestrates
    Backend --> SDK : provides
    SDK ..> Agent : used by
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Idle
    Idle --> Crawling : start_crawl
    Crawling --> Parsing : fetch_data
    Parsing --> Storing : parse_results
    Storing --> Idle : commit
    Crawling --> Error : exception
    Parsing --> Error : exception
    Error --> Idle : recover
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant U as User
    participant CLI as CLI
    participant A as Agent
    participant C as Crawler
    participant B as Backend
    U->>CLI: invoke crawl
    CLI->>A: request start
    A->>C: run crawler
    C->>B: store results
    B->>CLI: acknowledge
    CLI->>U: done
```
